	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt') != 'cffd85d6c48e0e80992b64887d665a6ff9c70330') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt') !== 'cffd85d6c48e0e80992b64887d665a6ff9c70330') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt') !== '64ecf97d643f4fdbcbe08b018c067cc4c938b9c0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt') !== 'cffd85d6c48e0e80992b64887d665a6ff9c70330') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/rfc/draft-viathinksoft-oidwhois.txt');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 524\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 524') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
